1  5this ansi is dedicated to my old pal, catch 22.   the guy who garnered        
5  respect from everyone in the scene for the integrity behind his group         
5  glue, his artwork, and just for being an all around cool motherfucker.        
5  priort to the spring 2013 blocktronics pack, glue was the last group i        
5  was in before shipping off to college.  i'm not sure if i knew it at the      
5  time, but i only released once in glue, and then that was that.  the only     
5  piece i had in the pack was a font, with me rambling on and on about how      
5  much the font sucks.  (a common thing for me to do)  anyway, years and        
5  years later i saw that ansi, and i thought to myself 'you are a fucking       
5  dumb motherfucker.'  my ONE release in glue is filled with me complaining     
5  about a shitty font.  it looked like inviting someone over for a nice         
5  dinner and they bring an apple pie the found in a dumpster and say "well,     
5  here's what i brought to your nice dinner.  a shitty dumpster pie."           
5  ugh, anyway - that didn't sit well with me when i saw that font years later.  
5  so that's why i'd like to give a shout ot to catch 22 (unfortunately i have   
5  yet to see hanging around.) in hopes that some day he sees this.
